[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mReport[0m===                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         # Evaluation Report                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Summary                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         A critical file path traversal vulnerability has been detected in the Apache Tika   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         codebase during fuzzing. The vulnerability occurs when processing embedded          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         documents through the RUnpackExtractor and FileSystemEmitter components, allowing   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         potential access to files outside the intended output directory through path        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         traversal sequences [1m([0me.g., `..[35m/[0m`[1m)[0m.                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ### Vulnerability Type                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         This is a **File Path Traversal** vulnerability [1m([0malso known as Directory            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Traversal[1m)[0m, classified as a critical security issue by the Jazzer fuzzing           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         sanitizer. Path traversal vulnerabilities allow attackers to access files and       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         directories stored outside the intended directory by manipulating file path inputs  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         with special character sequences.                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ### Issue Details                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         The security issue was triggered during fuzzing with the following characteristics: [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m. **Detected Path**: The traversal attempt targeted                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[35m/tmp/expander-tmp11025714002712459292/output/q/r/s/t/./input.bin/../../../[0m[95mjazzer-t[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [95mraversal[0m`                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The path contains both relative path components [1m([0m`.[35m/[0m`[1m)[0m and parent directory    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         references [1m([0m`..[35m/[0m`[1m)[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The traversal sequences attempt to navigate three levels up from the intended  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         output directory                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m. **Call Stack Analysis**:                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The vulnerability is detected by `[1;35mFilePathTraversal.check[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` in the Jazzer     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         sanitizer                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The issue originates in `[1;35mFileSystemEmitter.emit[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` at line [1;36m155[0m, which is       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         responsible for writing extracted content to the filesystem                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The malicious path is processed through                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[1;35mEmittingEmbeddedDocumentBytesHandler.add[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` when handling embedded documents       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The extraction chain starts with `RUnpackExtractor`, which parses R archive    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         formats and extracts embedded content                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m. **Execution Flow**:                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Document parsing begins through `TikaCLI` → `RecursivelyExtract` →             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `PipesServer`                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The `RecursiveParserWrapper` invokes the `AutoDetectParser` and                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `CompositeParser`                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The `PackageParser` handles the archive processing, iterating through entries  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - `[1;35mRUnpackExtractor.parseEmbedded[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` extracts content and stores bytes via       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[1;35mstoreEmbeddedBytes[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m`                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Finally, `[1;35mFileSystemEmitter.emit[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` attempts to write the extracted content to [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         disk                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ### Areas for Investigation                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         To obtain a holistic view of this vulnerability, the following components should be [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         investigated:                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m. **FileSystemEmitter [1m([0morg.apache.tika.pipes.emitter.fs[1m)[0m**:                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Line [1;36m155[0m where the emit operation occurs                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Path validation and sanitization logic before file write operations            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - How output paths are constructed and whether they properly validate            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         user-controlled input                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m. **EmittingEmbeddedDocumentBytesHandler**:                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - How embedded document names/paths are processed at line [1;36m66[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Whether filename metadata from archives is trusted without validation          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m. **RUnpackExtractor [1m([0morg.apache.tika.extractor[1m)[0m**:                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Methods `[1;35mstoreEmbeddedBytes[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` [1m([0mline [1;36m153[0m[1m)[0m and `[1;35mparseWithBytes[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` [1m([0mline [1;36m122[0m[1m)[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - How embedded file paths are extracted from R archives                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Whether archive entry names are used directly without sanitization             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m. **PackageParser [1m([0morg.apache.tika.parser.pkg[1m)[0m**:                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Entry parsing logic in `[1;35mparseEntry[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` [1m([0mline [1;36m481[0m[1m)[0m and `[1;35mparseEntries[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` [1m([0mline    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m386[0m[1m)[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - How entry names from archives are passed to downstream handlers                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m. **Path Construction and Validation**:                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The overall architecture for constructing output file paths when extracting    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         embedded documents                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Any existing path sanitization or validation mechanisms                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Configuration of output directories and how relative paths are resolved        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         The vulnerability appears to stem from insufficient validation of file paths        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         extracted from archive entries before using them to write files to the filesystem,  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         potentially allowing maliciously crafted archives to write files outside the        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         intended extraction directory.                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Initial Issue Log                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m77[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m78[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[39m**[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m79[0m[39m:     * This is a duplication of the algorithm and functionality[0m                  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m83[0m[39m:     * <p>[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m84[0m[39m:     * The goal of this is to get a filename from a path.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m85[0m[39m:     * The package parsers and some other embedded doc[0m                           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m90[0m[39m:     * bad things could happen.  Consider: [0m[32m"../../../my_ppt.ppt"[0m[39m.[0m                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m92[0m[39m:     * Consider using this in combination with [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m@link #[0m[1;35mnormalize[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m93[0m[39m:     *[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m95[0m[39m:     * @return empty string or a filename, never null[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m96[0m[39m:     *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m97[0m[39m:    public static String [0m[1;35mgetName[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal String path[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m98[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m99[0m[39m:        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpath == null || [0m[1;35mpath.isEmpty[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis Summary[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter analyzing the code snippets and evaluation report, I've identified the root [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcause and the optimal fix strategy for this critical path traversal vulnerability.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability originates in **[0m[1;35mPackageParser.handleEntryMetadata[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m** at line [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m223[0m[39m, where archive entry names are set directly into metadata without sanitization:[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mname = [0m[1;35mname.replace[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"\\", "[0m[35m/[0m[39m"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Line [0m[1;36m222[0m[39m - only replaces backslashes[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mentrydata.set[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTikaCoreProperties.RESOURCE_NAME_KEY, name[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Line [0m[1;36m223[0m[39m - [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mVULNERABLE[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis unsanitized name flows through:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. [0m[1;35mRUnpackExtractor.storeEmbeddedBytes[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m → [0m[1;35membeddedDocumentBytesHandler.add[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. [0m[1;35mEmittingEmbeddedDocumentBytesHandler.add[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m → [0m[1;35mgetEmitKey[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. [0m[1;35mAbstractEmbeddedDocumentBytesHandler.getEmitKey[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m → constructs path using [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munsanitized RESOURCE_NAME_KEY[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. [0m[1;35mFileSystemEmitter.emit[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m → [0m[1;35mbasePath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with malicious path containing[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"../"[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Evidence from Codebase[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe codebase already has multiple examples of proper sanitization:[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **UnrarParser** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m131[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m133[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Demonstrates the correct pattern:[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```java[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   String fName = [0m[1;35mFilenameUtils.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[39mrelPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;35mmetadata.set[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTikaCoreProperties.RESOURCE_NAME_KEY, fName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;35mmetadata.set[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTikaCoreProperties.ORIGINAL_RESOURCE_NAME, relPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **[0m[1;35mFilenameUtils.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m97[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m112[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Explicitly designed to prevent path [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtraversal with documentation warning about [0m[32m"../../../my_ppt.ppt"[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **TikaCLI and UnpackerResource**: Both implement multi-layer sanitization for [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39membedded file names[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Fix Strategy[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Primary Fix: Sanitize at the Root Cause [0m[1;39m([0m[39mPackageParser.handleEntryMetadata[0m[1;39m)[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location**: [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tika-parsers/tika-parsers-standard/tika-parsers-standard-modules/tika-parser-pkg-m[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39module/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/parser/pkg/PackageParser.java`[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Lines to modify**: [0m[1;36m221[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m231[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Changes**:[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Import `org.apache.tika.io.FilenameUtils` at the top of the file[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Replace lines [0m[1;36m221[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m231[0m[39m with sanitization logic:[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mname != null && [0m[1;35mname.length[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m > [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Normalize path separators[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    name = [0m[1;35mname.replace[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"\\", "[0m[35m/[0m[39m"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Sanitize the name to extract only the filename, preventing path traversal[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    String sanitizedName = [0m[1;35morg.apache.tika.io.FilenameUtils.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m If sanitization results in empty string [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., name was [0m[32m".."[0m[39m or [0m[32m"."[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m generate a safe default name[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39msanitizedName == null || [0m[1;35msanitizedName.isEmpty[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        sanitizedName = [0m[32m"file"[0m[39m;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Set sanitized name in RESOURCE_NAME_KEY[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mentrydata.set[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTikaCoreProperties.RESOURCE_NAME_KEY, sanitizedName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Preserve original path for reference/debugging purposes[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mentrydata.set[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTikaCoreProperties.ORIGINAL_RESOURCE_NAME, name[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Use sanitized name for HTML attributes[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    AttributesImpl attributes = new [0m[1;35mAttributesImpl[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mattributes.addAttribute[0m[1;39m([0m[32m""[0m[39m, [0m[32m"class"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"class"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"CDATA"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"embedded"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mattributes.addAttribute[0m[1;39m([0m[32m""[0m[39m, [0m[32m"id"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"id"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"CDATA"[0m[39m, sanitizedName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mxhtml.startElement[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"div"[0m[39m, attributes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Secondary Fix: Defense-in-Depth [0m[1;39m([0m[39mFileSystemEmitter path validation[0m[1;39m)[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location**: [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tika-pipes/tika-emitters/tika-emitter-fs/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/pipes/emitt[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mer/fs/FileSystemEmitter.java`[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Lines to modify**: [0m[1;36m145[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m165[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39memit method with InputStream[0m[1;39m)[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Changes**:[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAdd path validation after resolving the path, similar to FileSystemFetcher:[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m@Override[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpublic void [0m[1;35memit[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString path, InputStream inputStream, Metadata userMetadata, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mParseContext parseContext[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException, TikaEmitterException [0m[1;39m{[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbasePath == null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        throw new [0m[1;35mTikaEmitterException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"basePath must be configured"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    Path target = [0m[1;35mbasePath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Validate that the resolved path is still within basePath [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdefense-in-depth[0m[1;39m)[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    try [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        Path realTarget = [0m[1;35mtarget.toRealPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        Path realBase = [0m[1;35mbasePath.toRealPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mrealTarget.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mrealBase[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            throw new [0m[1;35mTikaEmitterException[0m[1;39m([0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                [0m[32m"Path escapes base directory. Path: "[0m[39m + path[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mIOException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m If toRealPath fails [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfile doesn't exist yet[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, validate the normalized [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpath[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        Path normalizedTarget = [0m[1;35mtarget.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.toAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        Path normalizedBase = [0m[1;35mbasePath.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.toAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mnormalizedTarget.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnormalizedBase[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            throw new [0m[1;35mTikaEmitterException[0m[1;39m([0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                [0m[32m"Path escapes base directory. Path: "[0m[39m + path[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mFiles.isDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtarget.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtarget.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[33m...[0m[39m rest of the existing code[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Also apply similar validation to the other [0m[1;35memit[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m method at lines [0m[1;36m77[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m98[0m[39m**:[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m@Override[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpublic void [0m[1;35memit[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString emitKey, List<Metadata> metadataList, ParseContext [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparseContext[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException, TikaEmitterException [0m[1;39m{[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[33m...[0m[39m existing null checks [0m[33m...[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfileExtension != null && [0m[1;35mfileExtension.length[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m > [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        emitKey += [0m[32m"."[0m[39m + fileExtension;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    Path output;[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbasePath != null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        output = [0m[1;35mbasePath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39memitKey[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Validate path [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdefense-in-depth[0m[1;39m)[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        try [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            Path realOutput = [0m[1;35moutput.toRealPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            Path realBase = [0m[1;35mbasePath.toRealPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mrealOutput.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mrealBase[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                throw new [0m[1;35mTikaEmitterException[0m[1;39m([0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                    [0m[32m"Path escapes base directory. EmitKey: "[0m[39m + emitKey[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mIOException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            Path normalizedOutput = [0m[1;35moutput.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.toAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            Path normalizedBase = [0m[1;35mbasePath.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.toAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mnormalizedOutput.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnormalizedBase[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                throw new [0m[1;35mTikaEmitterException[0m[1;39m([0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                    [0m[32m"Path escapes base directory. EmitKey: "[0m[39m + emitKey[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        output = [0m[1;35mPaths.get[0m[1;39m([0m[39memitKey[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[33m...[0m[39m rest of the existing code[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Justification[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why this is the optimal approach**:[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Fixes Root Cause**: The primary fix in [0m[1;35mPackageParser.handleEntryMetadata[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprevents malicious paths from ever entering the metadata system, protecting ALL [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdownstream consumers[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Follows Existing Patterns**: The fix uses the same pattern already implemented[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min UnrarParser and recommended in FilenameUtils documentation[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Defense-in-Depth**: The secondary fix in FileSystemEmitter provides an [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39madditional security layer, following the pattern already used in FileSystemFetcher[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Preserves Functionality**: [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Uses RESOURCE_NAME_KEY for sanitized filenames [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexisting behavior[0m[1;39m)[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Adds ORIGINAL_RESOURCE_NAME to preserve original paths if needed for debugging[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Maintains compatibility with all existing code paths[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **No Dependency Changes**: Uses only Tika's own FilenameUtils, not external [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCommons IO[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **Comprehensive Protection**: Handles all edge cases:[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Path traversal sequences [0m[1;39m([0m[32m"../"[0m[1;39m)[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Mixed path separators [0m[1;39m([0m[32m"\\" and "[0m[35m/[0m[39m"[0m[1;39m)[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Special filenames [0m[1;39m([0m[32m"."[0m[39m, [0m[32m".."[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Empty or null results from sanitization[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential Side Effects**:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Archive entries with directory paths in names will have only the filename [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextracted[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Existing code relying on full paths in RESOURCE_NAME_KEY may need updates[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Mitigation**:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The ORIGINAL_RESOURCE_NAME metadata field preserves the original path for any [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode that needs it[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. This aligns with security best practices - RESOURCE_NAME_KEY should contain only[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfilenames[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. The codebase already has examples [0m[1;39m([0m[39mUnrarParser[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m using this pattern successfully[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Testing Considerations[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix should support the same fuzzing logic without modifications to harness [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode. The fuzzer will:[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Still be able to create archives with malicious entry names[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Still trigger the parsing and extraction flow[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Now receive sanitized filenames instead of path traversal sequences[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Verify that files are written only within the intended output directory[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
